 Chinese troops entered the DBO sector about three weeks ago
 yah jaankaree aadhikarik sutron ne di
 On April 15, the Chinese Army, armed with about 50 vehicles and dogs, had penetrated 19 km inside the Indian border across the Line of Actual Control (LAC) in the DBO sector and buried five tents
 bhartiya sena ne bhi chini sena kii ore rukh karke 300 meter kii duuri par apane tent gaad die the
 There were four flag meetings between the military of the two countries
 shanivaar ko bhi ek flag meeting hui

 ham sabhi ke gharon main lakdi ke bartanon kaa istemaal kiya jaataa he
 Food is not made in these utensils but they are used for serving and eating
 lakdi ke in bartanon ko sahi rakh-rakhaav kii bahut jarurat hoti he
 In the absence of proper maintenance, they go bad and they smell bad
 aamtaur par lakdi ke bartanon ko dho dene ke baad bhi unamem se gandh jaati nahin he
 In such a situation, by trying these home remedies, you can get clean and odor-free utensils
 neembu kaa ras, sirka or baking soda se saaf karne par in bartanon kii gandhachali jaati he
 Clean wooden utensils with these home remedies: 1
 neembu:lakdi ke bartanon ko saaf karne ke liye neembu ke ras kaa istemaal karnaa sabase acha rahata he
 Mix a few drops of lemon in warm water
 iske baad bartanon ko isamen dubokar 15 minute ke liye yun hi chhod dijie
 When the water cools down, add some amount of hot water to it again
 15 minute tak ise yun hi chhod den or uske baad bartan ko baahar nikaal len
 Use the utensil after wiping it with a dry cloth
 2
 Vinegar: Mix half a bowl of vinegar in a bowl and keep it
 isamen ek chammach shahad mila lijie
 After that, squeeze a large piece of cotton into this solution
 is coton ball kii madad se bartan ko acchhee tarah ragadkar ponch lijie
 Doing this two to three times will remove the smell of the pot
 3
 Salt: Take hot water in a large bowl
 is garm pani main chaar se paanch chammach namak mila len
 Dip the wooden utensil in it and leave it for a while
 paanch se das minute tak bartan ko isi ghol main rahane dijie
 After taking it out, wipe it with a dry cloth
 4
 Baking Soda: Mix baking soda and lemon juice together and prepare a paste
 is paste ko lakdi ke bartan par lagaakar kuch der ke liye chhod dijie
 After that clean the pot with hot water
